On 2/8, slight GI issues, no body aches, and slight headache persist.

40 2021-02-25 nervousness Within one minute of receiving vaccine, the patient became pale, stated that he felt dizzy and faint... Read more
Close
Within one minute of receiving vaccine, the patient became pale, stated that he felt dizzy and fainted. Patient regained consciousness within one minute. Upon regaining consciousness, patient reported feeling lightheaded and dizzy but was oriented to person, place and time. Skin was warm and dry but pale in color. After regaining consciousness, patient also stated that he has a history of fainting 5-6 years ago after receiving an influenza vaccination. (During screening questions, patient denied having any reactions to vaccines in the past) Patient independently moved from a chair to a laying down position on a cot and expressed an improvement in how he was feeling. Vital signs taken after event as recorded below. When asked patient stated that he does recall times when he thinks he may have been hypoglycemic in the past. Patient also states that he has been very nervous about receiving injections throughout his life. EMS called and assessed patient at the vaccination clinic site. Patient drank a 10 oz bottle of orange juice prior to EMS arriving and when EMS staff obtained his blood sugar the result was 97. EMS stated that patient was stable and all vital signs were stable. Patients skin color improved to pink. Patients wife was called by patient and she provided transportation home for patient. Prior to leaving the vaccination clinic, patient was walking around for several minutes and denied any feelings of being lightheaded or dizzy. VITALS SIGNS: 5:06pm: Heart rate: 50, Oxygen Saturation: 99% on room air 5:15 pm: Blood pressure: 100/78 ; Heart rate: 50; oxygen saturation 99% on room air. 5:20pm: Blood pressure 98/76 Heart rate:52; oxygen saturation 96% on room air. 5:34 pm: Blood pressure 92/68 Heart rate: 53 oxygen saturation 97% on room air. Vital signs taken by EMS staff were not recorded by public health nursing staff.

Gen: Awake, Alert, Moderate Distress, diaphoretic Cardio: RRR w/o m/g/r Resp: LCAT in all fields, mildly increased work of breathing Skin: no rashes noted, no edema noted of the face or angioedema noted of the lips Psych: anxious Neuro: able to answer questions appropriately, able to follow instructions, CN 2-12 grossly intact Pt instructed that his symptoms were not necessarily consistent with anaphylaxis but with diaphoresis and left sided CP I recommended that he be evaluated in the Emergency Department. 40 2021-03-11 anxiety Patient felt to be in distress at the close of his observation time. He was complaining of trouble w... Read more
Close
Patient felt to be in distress at the close of his observation time. He was complaining of trouble with focusing his eyes, left sided chest pain, and was diaphoretic. Pt appeared to be in moderate distress and very anxious. I examined the pt through the car window and listened to his heart and lungs. Pt was not in respiratory distress and heart rate and rhythm were regular. Reassurance was provided to the pt, but he was also told that to be safe I recommended that he be evaluated in the emergency department and that he be transported via ambulance. Pt expressed understanding and agreed to going to the ED but was refusing transport via EMS. Pt was the passenger in the vehicle and he said that the driver could just take him. I expressed that transport via EMS would be the safest but we could not make him go via EMS and that if they wanted to leave via private vehicle then they could but i still recommended that he be evaluated in the ED. He expressed understanding and that he would go directly to the ED via personal car.
40 2021-03-16 feeling abnormal, disturbance in attention, insomnia It has been 6 weeks since my 2nd dose of the Moderna vaccine for Covid-19. For the first 3-4 days I ... Read more
Close
It has been 6 weeks since my 2nd dose of the Moderna vaccine for Covid-19. For the first 3-4 days I had the usual moderate flu-like symptoms: dizziness, headaches, fatigue, chills, soreness at vaccine siteetc. Days 5-7 I seemed to gradually improve. On day 8 all of the symptoms returned with greater severity: this time I had a fever, the chills were much more intense, the headaches were excruciating, body and joint aches all over the place--I couldn't sleep or focus on anything cognitively taxing. Interestingly, my brother, who was vaccinated just after me, also had more severe side effects beginning on day 8 post 2nd dose. He improved after 3-4 days, but my recovery has been much much lengthier. By day 14 I was still feeling very ill, though the fever did subside. Sometime in the third week the pain in my arm at the vaccination site returned, then became intermittent, and still bothers me from time to time. I also started getting muscle spasms in the same exact locations that sent me to the ER after my probably bout with Covid in the spring of 2020. Thankfully these lasted only a week or so, though I began feeling muscle soreness in different parts of my body, ever changing. By the 4th week I was slightly better and down to 4 main symptoms: chills (by far the worst of the symptoms--to the point at which my skin would feel like it was being frostbitten by dry ice every time I changed sweaty clothes), occasional splitting headaches, and muscle soreness that included both the injection site on my arm and other areas. I had other symptoms as well, fatigue and brain fog, etc, but these were present before the vaccination, though not as severe.

"Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine EUA" Several hours after receiving first dose of vaccine my left arm became very painful to the point of bringing me to tears whenever I tried to move it or use it: lifting something as simple as a glass of water was excruciating pain. Second day is a little better with a little more mobility, but trying to undress and undress is torture, especially lifting my arm over my head or past my chest.

40 2021-03-23 impaired work ability, anxiety, excessive sleepiness Initial symptoms of the first shot included injection site pain, neck soreness, and severe headache ... Read more
Close
Initial symptoms of the first shot included injection site pain, neck soreness, and severe headache that would come and go. The next day I was so exhausted I couldn't work for 2 days. I barely got out of bed until about 40 hours after the shot where I was able to get out and do some gardening. The reason I am filling this out was at right around 72 hours after the vaccine, I was laying down watching a YouTube video feeling quite relaxed. I then experienced a tachycardia event where my heart rate went up to 120 and stayed there for about an hour. I remained calm and was not experiencing anxiety, but the heart rate persisted. I have had this happen before in panic attacks, but it's quite rare and I am in acute, high level stress. Almost 2 weeks later to the day, I had another tachycardia, stronger than any I've had my entire life that only lasted about 7 seconds, but I would estimate my heart rate jumped to over 250. I thought I was going to go into cardiac arrest it was so jarring. I'm not sure if that one was related to the vaccine.

40 2021-04-12 sleep disorder, impaired work ability, loss of personal independence in daily activities On 4/8/21 awoke to intense pain in his left foot about 12 hours after receiving his 1st dose Moderna... Read more
Close
On 4/8/21 awoke to intense pain in his left foot about 12 hours after receiving his 1st dose Moderna vaccine batch #038B21A. Over the next few days swelling and pain increased in the left foot moving around from the big toe, to ankle, to arch. His foot was swollen and extremely painful and he was not able to walk or put weight on the foot. On 4/18 he went to the clinic. The doctor took fluid from the big toe joint to test uric acid levels. Elevated levels of uric acid confirmed his condition to be Gout and Indomethacin was prescribed for pain and swelling. He has never had Gout or any kind of arthritis, joint pain or foot injury prior to the Moderna vaccine. As of 4/13/21 he is still unable to walk or sleep well due to pain and swelling in the foot. He is not able to work or resume normal daily activities.
40 2021-04-17 anxiety, depression What a nightmare. Moderna shot #1 caused rapid hair loss and arm soreness for a week and low grade n... Read more
Close
What a nightmare. Moderna shot #1 caused rapid hair loss and arm soreness for a week and low grade nausea. But shot #2, holy moly... 12 hours post shot, I developed a fever, chills, violent shaking much of the night, weight loss, nausea, kept throwing up, massive migraine, heart rate racing, every cell in my body throbbing in pain, difficulty urinating, simply staying alive was exhausting. It faded a couple days after the shot, and in its place, fatigue, difficulty getting a full breath in. And now I have tinnitus--constant ear ringing. Absolute torture. And of course significantly more hair loss. So let's add anxiety and depression to the list because of this hell. What a regret it was to get injected with this poison. Rather just keep masking and avoiding people than be stuck with these permanent, life debilitating problems. I know it wont change anything, but I figure I'd report it anyway. What a nightmare. This crap should not be given to anyone with an autoimmune disorder.

On 25FEB2021, the patient started having a headache and on 26FEB2021 the paralysis on the left side of the face began. The patient said that they were experiencing fibromyalgia and neuropathy that they had when they had cancer. Note: I had a PCR confirmed SARS-CoV-2 infection in March, 2020. Approximately 12 hours after the second vaccine dose, I experienced intense soreness at the vaccination site (significantly greater than the first dose). In the middle of the night I awoke with flu-like symptoms. At 9am I took acetominophen for fever, rigors, muscle aches. This brought mild relief from approx. 9:45am to 11:15 am. My condition continued to worsen through the early afternoon with rigors and significant generalized muscle aches. I experienced tachycardia (90-105 bpm vs normal of ~70bpm), SOB, and starting measuring pulse oximetry which read from 89%-94% (my usual does not go below 97%). This persisted until approximately 8pm with no improvement. I took 40 mg prednisone, 600 mg ibuprofen and within 3 hours was starting to have symptom resolution. I am a physician and up to date on all my vaccinations. I have never had anything approaching this type of response. I don't know if prior SARS-CoV-2 infection creates a situation were the very potent mRNA vaccine triggers a large immunologic recall response. I wanted to get this noted as there may be some reason to alter the vaccine schedule for prior SARS-CoV-2 infections

Close
On 2/23/21, about 12 days after the vaccine was received, I felt chest pains in the late afternoon. At midnight, I woke up with uncontrollable chills and shakes, with a low-grade fever that hovered in the 99.5 -100 range. I attempted to get up and struggled to breathe,; it was as if my abdominal and lower back muscles were seizing. I had to crawl to a kneeling position to urinate. I took several Tylenol then went back to lie down; after a few hours, the fever subsided, and I was able to briefly fall back asleep. At 4:00 a.m. the fever and major chills subsided, with no fevers reported since then, and only occasional chills. However, the muscle fatigue, pain and stiffness have become frighteningly debilitating. On Wednesday - Friday, the three days after I first experienced symptoms, each day it took me between 1.5 - 2 hours to get out of bed and finally get to a standing position. During the day on each day following my first symptoms, I have been able to gradually walk around, go up and down stairs, use the bathroom, and perform basic tasks. However, when the evening comes, it is a different story. 12 midnight - 10 a.m. are the worst hours, as any extended period lying down results in my muscles seizing, freezing and stiffening up. After falling asleep for an hour, it takes 10-20 minutes to mobilize enough (using a crutch and assistance) to get to the bathroom. After falling asleep for 2-3 hours, it takes 30-40 minutes to do the same. And, if I fall asleep for 3+ hours (which is about as long as I've been able to sleep since the adverse reactions began), it will take 1.5 - 2 hours to get completely mobile. This is when I finally wake for the day, and it takes about 10 minutes to raise my head and turn my torso, then another 10-15 minutes to get my legs off the bed and assume a crouching position, then 30-60 minutes to stand on my own.

I am scheduled to get the second shot on Friday, March 26, at a vaccination site, State University.

50 2021-03-20 excessive sleepiness I don't think that my reaction to the vaccine is super serious but it is perhaps worth noting if oth... Read more
Close
I don't think that my reaction to the vaccine is super serious but it is perhaps worth noting if others are also experiencing similar symptoms. On the second day, I did have the expected arm soreness around the injection area on my right arm. That soreness faded by Saturday morning. However, on Saturday afternoon, I began experiencing some intermittent pain in my left kidney. I have had a few (3?) kidney stones since I was approximately 35 years old so it is a pain that I recognize almost immediately. I kept my spider senses awake to see where it was going to go. About an hour later, I had intermittent "flu like" pain in my arms and legs. I had been up on a ladder painting a wall and I became a bit dizzy and decided to halt the painting project. The rest of the evening was kind of crappy. Intermittent headaches, leg pain, arm pain and left kidney pain. I took 1 Alleve tablet around 8pm. It didn't seem to do much. I took a second one about an hour later (according to the instructions you can take two for you first dose) and that seemed to do the trick! I slept like a rock and so far today, all of the pain is gone including the pain in my left kidney. I have not taken any more Alleve besides the two that I took last night. Also, as of right now (2:44pm on Sunday 3/21), no kidney stone has passed. I have been urinating into a cup to see if one comes out. I cannot 100% say that any of these symptoms are related to the vaccine. However, being a Type 1 diabetic (since 1978) and the unusual kidney pain made me go, "huh." That is why I am providing this info in the event that there are others who are experiencing similar symptoms that can be tied to the vaccine and what to expect. I feel completely fine now. Yay. :)

colon stenosis; unspecified disorder of intestine; dry skin; Laceration; Wound healing delayed; bruise; nightmares; general body pain; Muscle ache; fatigue; fever; chills; This spontaneous case was reported by a non-health professional and describes the occurrence of LARGE INTESTINAL STENOSIS (colon stenosis) in a 56-year-old male patient who received mRNA-1273 (Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine) for COVID-19 vaccination. The occurrence of additional non-serious events is detailed below. Co-suspect product included non-company product ADALIMUMAB (HUMIRA) injection for an unknown indication. The patient's past medical history included Stomach pain, Diarrhea (two to three formed stools per day), Constipation and Surgery (Surgery to remove affected portions of his intestines.) in 1991. On 23-Jun-2020, the patient started ADALIMUMAB (HUMIRA) (unknown route) 40 mg. On an unknown date, the patient received first dose of mRNA-1273 (Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine) (Intramuscular) 1 dosage form. On an unknown date, received second dose of mRNA-1273 (Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine) (Intramuscular) dosage was changed to 1 dosage form. On an unknown date, the patient experienced LARGE INTESTINAL STENOSIS (colon stenosis) (seriousness criterion medically significant), GASTROINTESTINAL DISORDER (unspecified disorder of intestine), DRY SKIN (dry skin), SKIN LACERATION (Laceration), IMPAIRED HEALING (Wound healing delayed), CONTUSION (bruise), NIGHTMARE (nightmares), PAIN (general body pain), MYALGIA (Muscle ache), FATIGUE (fatigue), PYREXIA (fever) and CHILLS (chills). At the time of the report, LARGE INTESTINAL STENOSIS (colon stenosis), GASTROINTESTINAL DISORDER (unspecified disorder of intestine), DRY SKIN (dry skin), SKIN LACERATION (Laceration), IMPAIRED HEALING (Wound healing delayed), CONTUSION (bruise), NIGHTMARE (nightmares), PAIN (general body pain), MYALGIA (Muscle ache), FATIGUE (fatigue), PYREXIA (fever) and CHILLS (chills) outcome was unknown. The patient received both scheduled doses of mRNA-1273 prior to the events therefore, action taken with the drug in response to the events was not applicable. Company comment: Very limited information regarding this events has been provided at this time. Further information has been requested.; Sender's Comments: Very limited information regarding this events has been provided at this time. Further information has been requested.

Colon stenosis; Unspecified disorder of intestine; Post-procedural pain; Surgical scar; Laceration; Wound healing delayed; Bruise; Nighmare; Chills; Muscle aches; Fever; Fatigue; This spontaneous case was reported by a physician (subsequently medically confirmed) and describes the occurrence of LARGE INTESTINAL STENOSIS (Colon stenosis) in a 56-year-old male patient who received mRNA-1273 (Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine) for COVID-19 vaccination. The occurrence of additional non-serious events is detailed below. Co-suspect product included non-company product ADALIMUMAB (HUMIRA) for Crohn's disease. No Medical History information was reported. On an unknown date, the patient received second dose of mRNA-1273 (Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine) (Intramuscular) 1 dosage form and ADALIMUMAB (HUMIRA) (Subcutaneous) 1 dosage form. On an unknown date, the patient experienced LARGE INTESTINAL STENOSIS (Colon stenosis) (seriousness criterion medically significant), GASTROINTESTINAL DISORDER (Unspecified disorder of intestine), PROCEDURAL PAIN (Post-procedural pain), SCAR (Surgical scar), SKIN LACERATION (Laceration), IMPAIRED HEALING (Wound healing delayed), CONTUSION (Bruise), NIGHTMARE (Nighmare), CHILLS (Chills), MYALGIA (Muscle aches), PYREXIA (Fever) and FATIGUE (Fatigue). At the time of the report, LARGE INTESTINAL STENOSIS (Colon stenosis), GASTROINTESTINAL DISORDER (Unspecified disorder of intestine), PROCEDURAL PAIN (Post-procedural pain), SCAR (Surgical scar), SKIN LACERATION (Laceration), IMPAIRED HEALING (Wound healing delayed) and CONTUSION (Bruise) had not resolved and NIGHTMARE (Nighmare), CHILLS (Chills), MYALGIA (Muscle aches), PYREXIA (Fever) and FATIGUE (Fatigue) had resolved. For mRNA-1273 (Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine) (Intramuscular), the reporter did not provide any causality assessments. No concomitant medicines were reported. No treatment information were reported. Action taken with the drug in response to events was not applicable. Very limited information regarding these events has been provided at this time. The events are probably related to the patient's comorbidities. A causal relationship cannot be excluded for the events of fatigue, chills, pyrexia, and myalgia. procedure in which his heart was cut from top to bottom/pacemaker dependent; fast heart rate; afib; red dots on both of his arms; rash on both arms; dizzy; sick; very weak/no energy; hard time walking; cannot do the simplest of tasks; flutter; A spontaneous report was received from a Consumer concerning herself, a 57-year-old male patient, who received Moderna's COVID-19 vaccine (mRNA-1273) and experienced the events, fast heart rate, cardiac pacemaker dependent, atrial fibrillation, red dots on both of his arms, rash on both arms, dizziness, sick, Atrial flutter, very weak and no energy, hard time walking, and cannot do the simplest of tasks. The patient's medical history included atrial fibrillation and had a pacemaker placed about 8-9 months ago. Products known to have been used by the patient, within two weeks prior to the event were blood pressure medication, antiarrhythmics. On 01 Mar 2021, prior to the onset of events, the patient received their first of the two planned doses of mRNA-1273 (Lot number: 030m20a) via unknown route for prophylaxis of COVID-19 infection. On 01 Mar 2021, after vaccination, the patient developed red dots on both of his arms. For next two days, the patient had rash on both arms, was dizzy, felt sick, developed fast heart rate; went to hospital twice for heart rate either 07 Mar 2021 or 13 Mar 2021.During first visit to hospital, fast rate was brought under control, while in the second visit, the patient had a procedure in which his heart was cut from top to bottom and was made pacemaker dependent. The atrial fibrillation could not be controlled for 26 hours and had a flutter which was not identified and could not be controlled. Flutter returned after stopping amlodipine and hence patient was restarted on amlodipine. The patient now feels very weak, has a hard time walking, has no energy, cannot do the simplest of tasks, still experiences fast heart rate and flutter every now and then. No Laboratory investigations were provided. The Treatment information included pacemaker, amlodipine. Action taken with mRNA-1273 in response to the events was not provided. The outcome of the events, fast heart rate, cardiac pacemaker dependent, atrial fibrillation, red dots on both of his arms, rash on both arms, dizziness, sick, atrial flutter, very weak and no energy, hard time walking, cannot do the simplest of tasks were unknown.

On 24-Mar-2021, the patient experienced SUICIDAL IDEATION (Suicidal thoughts) (seriousness criterion medically significant), TINNITUS (Both ears ringing, nonstop), INSOMNIA (Can't sleep), DECREASED APPETITE (No appetite), BODY TEMPERATURE FLUCTUATION (Either hot or cold, no in between/hot and cold sweats), FEELING ABNORMAL (Feels boxed in) and THINKING ABNORMAL (Having weird thoughts). He was not admitted. Caller stated that things are so bad that he even had suicidal thoughts and was prone to anxiety. Since 26-Mar-2021, his appetite had returned and the felling of hot, cold sweats had gone away. Treatment was not provided. Brought in from ED, family concerned for altered mental status, hyperthermia, Tmax in 105. The patient stated that after the covid-19 vaccine on Friday, he experienced acute onset of R shoulder pain, constant, associated with decreased ROM. On PM Monday, he noticed first episode of chills, that lasted a few minutes, accompanied with sweating. This episode recurred 4 times over the week, then the family started noticed the patient was unable to answer questions and was somnolent. Blood Cultures in the ED were positive for MRSA 2:2. He was positive for endocarditis (previous dental work). Acute metabolic encephalopathy due to severe sepsis most likely 2/2 MRSA bacteremia complicated by NSTEMI and AKI in setting of newly diagnosed aortic valve endocarditis complicated by septic emboli to the bilateral cerebral hemispheres

Chills and Muscle aches Started about 18 hrs after the shot. Muscle Aches, Chills and Fever for the next 12 hours. Overnight aches continued with Nausea and hard to sleep. They are finally under control 1 week later. I hope this helps.
59 2021-03-27 anxiety Vaccine was administered at 11:12 AM and at 11:14 AM the patient began to complain of "feeling funny... Read more
Close
Vaccine was administered at 11:12 AM and at 11:14 AM the patient began to complain of "feeling funny" further identified as clammy skin, visible perspiration on his neck and forehead, dizziness, anxious, tingling in legs and arms. After applying two ice packs to the patient's neck and forehead, instructing him to take deep breaths, and him drinking 2 bottles of cold water (approximately 15 minutes), the patient reported feeling like normal. He waited in the observation area for an additional 15 minutes until 11:45 and was driven home by his wife with reports of feeling fine.

59 2021-04-06 nervousness Husband and wife came in 4/5 and received their COVID vaccines at 11am. They waited the 15 minutes t... Read more
Close
Husband and wife came in 4/5 and received their COVID vaccines at 11am. They waited the 15 minutes to check for reactions and were unsymptomatic when time was up. The pharmacy did a courtesy call around 3:15 pm on 4/7 to check in with them and see how they were feeling. The wife stated that her husband had passed away the night of 4/5. Wife stated that they were getting ready to go to bed and husband felt hot and shaky so he laid in front of a fan. Wife eventually had to do CPR and stated that she thinks that he passed away during the time while they were waiting for EMS, which took about 45 minutes. Patient was pronounced dead night of 4/5. Wife stated that patient has a history of heart problems including hypertension and multiple stents place and that she does not think the vaccine had to do with her husband's death.
